<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gisprekki</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gasprakjÄ…</i>. ***gestaag.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gestaag.html>gestaag</a> (51847)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">gestadig</i> through syncope, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gestadich</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gestedich</i>. Prefixed from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ge-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">stadig</i>, although the unprefixed form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>steady, continuous</li>
<li>gradual</li></ol>

***gesundheit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gesundheit.html>gesundheit</a> (51842)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:gesundheit.html>Gesundheit</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span>literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€œ</span><span class="mention-gloss">health</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â€</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>
